### Post by thomas144 on 2010-03-26
I think that I did a good job on this. Maybe I'm just being arrogant.
```
 
<html>
<head>
<title>Ubuntu Rules!</title>
</head>
<body>
<!-- This used to be an apology for not using an Ubuntu font. Some Googling 
fixed that. I also included a Mac font. -->
<font face="times new roman,freeserif,helvetica,courier new,freemono" 
size="3" color="black">
I have a fair understanding of HTML thanks to <a 
href="http://www.ironspider.ca/">www.ironspider.ca</a><br>
My skills of HTML are not exactly wonderful, but I know enough to format some 
text. Oh, well. I'm not a Web designer, so I have no reason to worry. As of 
now, I'm just trying to take up space.<br>
<br>
If you were to copy this into a text editor (like gedit [for Ubuntu] or 
Notepad [for Windows]), and saved it as a .htm file, you would actually have 
a Web page. Pretty cool, huh?
<br><br><br><br>This is just for fun.<br><br>
<font face="calibri,arial,garuda" size="7" color="#FFB026">
ubuntu rules!
</font>
</body>
</html>

```

.ocolor, .ofont, .osize, .osmilie, .osyscoloar, .smilietitle {
	background: #FFFFFF;
	color: #000000;
	border: 1px solid #FFFFFF;
}

	border: 1px solid #FFFFFF;
}

	background: #FFFFFF;
	color: #000000;
	border-right: 1px solid #FFFFFF;
}

	background: #FFFFFF;
}

	background: #FFFFFF;
	color: #000000;
}

	border-left: 1px solid #F8F8F3;
}

{

	padding: 0px 2px 0px 2px;
	cursor: default;

	overflow: hidden;
}
